#!/bin/bash
sh-4.1$ source  /afs/cern.ch/cms/cmsset_default.sh
xml HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487_1_cfg.py || exit $? ; 
echo 100 events were ran 
grep "TotalEvents" HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487_rt.xml 
grep "Timing-tstoragefile-write-totalMegabytes" HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487_rt.xml 
grep "PeakValueRss" HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487_rt.xml 
grep "AvgEventTime" HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487_rt.xml 
grep "AvgEventCPU" HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487_rt.xml 
grep "TotalJobCPU" HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487_rt.xml 

sh-4.1$ export SCRAM_ARCH=slc6_amd64_gcc481
sh-4.1$ if [ -r CMSSW_7_1_16_patch1/src ] ; then 
>  echo release CMSSW_7_1_16_patch1 already exists
> else
> scram p CMSSW CMSSW_7_1_16_patch1
> fi
sh-4.1$ cd CMSSW_7_1_16_patch1/src
sh-4.1$ eval `scram runtime -sh`
sh-4.1$ 
sh-4.1$ curl -s --insecure https://cms-pdmv.cern.ch/mcm/public/restapi/requests/get_fragment/HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487 --retry 2 --create-dirs -o Configuration/GenProduction/python/HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487-fragment.py 
sh-4.1$ [ -s Configuration/GenProduction/python/HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487-fragment.py ] || exit $?;
sh-4.1$ 
sh-4.1$ scram b
>> Local Products Rules ..... started
>> Local Products Rules ..... done
>> Building CMSSW version CMSSW_7_1_16_patch1 ----
>> Entering Package Configuration/GenProduction
>> Creating project symlinks
  src/Configuration/GenProduction/python -> python/Configuration/GenProduction
>> Leaving Package Configuration/GenProduction

>> Creating project symlinks
  src/Configuration/GenProduction/python -> python/Configuration/GenProduction

>> Compiling python modules python

>> All python modules compiled
>> Pluging of all type refreshed.
>> Done generating edm plugin poisoned information
gmake[1]: Leaving directory `/tmp/rebeca/CMSSW_7_1_16_patch1'
sh-4.1$ cd ../../
sh-4.1$ cmsDriver.py Configuration/GenProduction/python/HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487-fragment.py --fileout file:HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487.root --mc --eventcontent LHE --datatier LHE --conditions MCRUN2_71_V1::All --step LHE --python_filename HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487_1_cfg.py --no_exec --customise Configuration/DataProcessing/Utils.addMonitoring -n 100 || exit $? ; 
LHE,ENDJOB
Step: LHE Spec: 
Loading lhe fragment from Configuration.GenProduction.HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487-fragment
Step: ENDJOB Spec: 
customising the process with addMonitoring from Configuration/DataProcessing/Utils
Config file HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487_1_cfg.py created
sh-4.1$ cmsRun -e -j HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487_rt.xml HIG-RunIIWinter15wmLHE-00487_1_cfg.py || exit $? ;

ih2 1             ! hadron 2 (1 for protons, -1 for antiprotons)

ebeam2 6500d0     ! energy of beam 2

! To be set only if using internal (mlm) pdfs

! To be set only if using different pdf sets for the two incoming hadrons

use-old-grid    1 ! if 1 use old grid if file pwggrids.dat is present (<> 1 regenerate)
use-old-ubound  1 ! if 1 use norm of upper bounding function stored in pwgubound.dat, if present; <> 1 regenerate

! the typical call uses 1/1400 seconds (1400 calls per second)
ncall1 300000      ! Number of calls for the construction of the importance sampling grid
itmx1 1           ! Number of iterations for grid
ncall2 300000      ! Number of calls for the computation of the upper bounding envelope
                  ! for the generation of radiation
itmx2 1           ! Number of iterations for the above
! Notice: the total number of calls is ncall2*itmx2*foldcsi*foldy*foldphi
foldcsi 2         ! number of folds on csi integration
foldy   5         ! number of folds on  y  integration
foldphi 2         ! number of folds on phi integration

nubound 2000000 ! number of calls to set up the upper bounding norms for radiation
               ! This is performed using only the Born cross section (fast)


! OPTIONAL PARAMETERS


#ptsqmin    0.8    ! (default 0.8 GeV) minimum pt for generation of radiation

#charmthrpdf  1.5  ! (default 1.5 GeV) pdf charm treshold
#bottomthrpdf 5.0  ! (default 5.0 GeV) pdf bottom treshold

#xupbound 2d0   ! increase upper bound for radiation generation
iseed    234567         !  Start the random number generator with seed iseed
#rand1     0          !  skipping  rand2*100000000+rand1 numbers.  
#rand2     0          !  (see RM48 short writeup in CERNLIB)
